$ vi package.json
 "scripts": {
        "bundle":"browserify index.js -o bundle.js"
  },

$ npm run bundle
> video@1.0.0 bundle /home/eric/Devel/JavaScript/Node/Browserify/video
> browserify index.js -o bundle.js

/ als we 
 "scripts": {
        "start":"browserify index.js -o bundle.js"
  },
/ dan hoeven we alleen	,
$ npm start	,

[eric@almond video]$ node index.js
/home/eric/Devel/JavaScript/Node/Browserify/video/index.js:2
	alert("Foo");
ReferenceError: alert is not defined
/ Klopt, dit is een client side fct	, 
/ Dus geef in chrome	,
file:///home/eric/Devel/JavaScript/Node/Browserify/video/index.html
/ OK

/ 13	. 

[eric@almond video]$ npm i jquery --save

[eric@almond video]$ cat  index.html 
<!doctype html>
<html>
<head>
</head>
<body>
	<script src="bundle.js"></script>
</body>
</html>

[eric@almond video]$ cat  index.js
+function(){
var $=require('jquery');
var button=$('<button>').html('Click me').on('click',function(){
	alert('Foo Bar');
});
$('body').append(button);
}();

/ Geef	,
file:///home/eric/Devel/JavaScript/Node/Browserify/video/index.html
/ OK

/ we add dynamically een button aan HTML	, we hoeven deze dus niet in HTML te write	,

/ 7	. 

/ OWN MODULE

/ See	, 
https://quickleft.com/blog/creating-and-publishing-a-node-js-module/
/ See	,
https://docs.npmjs.com/getting-started/creating-node-modules

/ 13	. 

/ Met	,
exports.button=button;

/ we maken een aparte module	, my 	, naast video	, met het button	, 
[eric@almond Browserify]$ pwd
/home/eric/Devel/JavaScript/Node/Browserify
[eric@almond Browserify]$ mkdir my
[eric@almond Browserify]$ cd my
[eric@almond my]$ npm init
[eric@almond my]$ npm i jquery --save
[eric@almond my]$ vi index.js 
var $=require('jquery');
var button=$('<button>').html('Click me').on('click',function(){
    alert('Foo Bar');
});
exports.button=button;

[eric@almond video]$ cat index2.html 
<!doctype html>
<html>
<head>
</head>
<body>
	<script src="bundle2.js"></script>
</body>
</html>

[eric@almond video]$ cat index2.js 
var $=require('jquery');
var my=require('my');
$('body').append(my.button);

/ Geef	,
file:///home/eric/Devel/JavaScript/Node/Browserify/video/index2.html
/ OK

/ Met	, 
exports.button=button;
/ kun je ook meerdere maken	, 
exports.input=input;
/ en je moet de module noemen in de importing script	, want dat hebben we nog niet gedaan	,

/ 13	. 

/ Met	, 
module.exports=button;

[eric@almond video]$ cat node_modules/my/index.js 
var $=require('jquery');
var button=$('<button>').html('Click me').on('click',function(){
	alert('Foo Bar');
});
module.exports=button;


[eric@almond video]$ cat index2.js
var $=require('jquery');
var button=require('my');
$('body').append(button);

[eric@almond video]$ npm run bundle2
/ Geef	,
file:///home/eric/Devel/JavaScript/Node/Browserify/video/index2.html
/ OK

/ require, module.exports zijn def in webpack/browserify	,  
/ Maar in Node kan het ook	, maar dat is server side	, 
/ we kunnen require, en module.exports NIET in browser use	,
/ Dus als we in express  een app maken	, dan kun je in server.js require, module.exports use	, maar niet in public/client.js , want die runs in browser	,

/ 13	. 

/ loaders in webpack.

/ Intermezzo

/ Lees,
https://webpack.github.io/docs/using-loaders.html

{
    module: {
        loaders: [
						{ test: /\.jade$/, loader: "jade" },
            // => "jade" loader is used for ".jade" files
            { test: /\.css$/, loader: "style!css" },
            // => "style" and "css" loader is used for ".css" files
            // Alternative syntax:
            { test: /\.css$/, loaders: ["style", "css"] },
        ]
    }
}
/ of met CLI	,
$ webpack --module-bind jade --module-bind 'css=style!css'

/ Einde Intermezzo

/ we doen	,

$ vi webpack.config.js
module.exports={
  entry:'./src/main.js',
  output:{
    path:'./bin',
    filename:'app.bundle.js'
  },
  module:{
    loaders:[
    {
      test:/\.js$/,
      include:/src/,
      loader:'babel-loader'
    },
    {
      test:/\.css$/,
      include:/src/,
      loader:'style!css'
    }
    ]
  }
}

$ vi src/bear.js
import $ from 'jquery';
export var elem=$('<div/>').text('grzzly growl').get(0)
import _ from './bear.css';

/ OK	,

/we kunnen ook 
$ vi webpack.config.js
  module:{
    loaders:[
    {
      test:/\.js$/,
      include:/src/,
      loader:'babel-loader'
    },
    {
      test:/\.css$/,
      include:/src/,
      loaders:['style','css']
    }
    ]
  }
/ Let op: loaders: ipv loader:	,

/ COMMONJS ES6 MODULES

/ commonJS is require , exports.module	, exports.<prop>
/ es6 is import , export	,

[eric@almond Usage]$ pwd
/home/eric/Devel/JavaScript/Node/Webpack/Docs/Usage

[eric@almond Usage]$ cat webpack.config.js 
module.exports={
	entry:'./src/main.js',
	output:{
...

/ 13	. 

/ require, module.exports	, exports.<prop>

[eric@almond Usage]$ cat src/main.js 
var bar=require('./bar');
console.log(bar);
var baz=require('./baz');
console.log(baz.baz);
console.log(baz.gee);

[eric@almond Usage]$ cat src/bar.js 
module.exports='bar';
[eric@almond Usage]$ cat src/baz.js 
exports.baz='baz';
exports.gee='gee';


eric@almond Usage]$ npm start
> webpack
app.bundle.js  302 bytes       0  [emitted]  main

[eric@almond Usage]$ node bin/app.bundle.js 
bar
baz
gee

/ Als we we een module module.exports use	, en exports.<prop>	, dan is deze laatste undefined , 
/ Dus exports.<prop> moet in aparte module	,
/ Als we in de bar module	, 
module.exports='bar'
exports.baz='baz'
/ en in main module	,
var bar=require('./bar');
var baz=require('./baz');
console.log(bar);
console.log(bar.baz);
/ dan zien we 
bar
undefined	,

/ 13	. 

/ import	, export

eric@almond Usage]$ cat webpack.config.js 
module.exports={
	entry:'./src/main2.js',
...

eric@almond Usage]$  cat src/main2.js 
import bar from './bar2';
console.log(bar);
import {baz} from './baz2';
console.log(baz);
import {gee} from './baz2';
console.log(gee);
import {hee} from './baz2';
console.log(hee());

[eric@almond Usage]$ cat src/bar2.js 
export default 'bar2';

[eric@almond Usage]$ cat src/baz2.js 
export var baz='baz';												/ var MOET	,
export var gee='gee';
export function hee(){
	return 'hee';
}

https://24ways.org/2014/javascript-modules-the-es6-way/

/ 13	. 

/ webpack.config.js

webpack is a very flexible module bundler. It offers a lot of advanced features, but not all features are exposed via the command-line interface. To gain full access to webpack’s flexibility, we need to create a “configuration file”.

[eric@almond Usage]$ mkdir src bin
[eric@almond Usage]$ mv app.js  cats.js src
[eric@almond Usage]$ rm app.bundle.js 

[eric@almond Usage]$ ls
bin  node_modules  package.json  src webpack.config.js

/ in node_modules/ is webpack	,

[eric@almond Usage]$ cat webpack.config.js 
module.exports={
	entry:'./src/app.js',
	output:{
		path:'./bin',
		filename:'app.bundle.js'
	}
};

A webpack configuration file is a CommonJS-style module. So you can run any kind of code here, as long as a configuration object is exported out of this module.

///////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
/ we gaan nu es2015 write	, geen JS 	, dus require verandert in import	,

webpack only supports JavaScript modules natively, but most people will be using a transpiler for ES2015, CoffeeScript, TypeScript, etc. They can be used in webpack by using loaders.

Loaders are special modules webpack uses to ‘load’ other modules (written in another language) into JavaScript (that webpack understands). For example, babel-loader uses Babel to load ES2015 files.

./App.js ------------>	babel-loader!./App.js
					babel-loader

json-loader loads JSON files (simply by prepending module.exports = to turn it into a CommonJs module).

./cats.json ------------>			json-loader!./cats.json
						json-loader
['dave','henry','martha'] 		module.exports=['dave','henry','martha']

./cats.yml	------------> yaml-loader!./cats.yml ------------------> json-loader!./cats.json

$ vi cats.js
var cats=['dave','henry','martha'];
/ WAS	,
//module.exports=cats;
// NU	,
export default cats;

$ vi app.js

/ WAS	,
var cats=require('./cats');
console.log(cats);
/ NU	,
import cats from './cats';
import $ from 'jquery';

$('<h1>Cats</h1>').appendTo('body');
const ul=$('<ul></ul>').appendTo('body');
for (const cat of cats){
  $('<li></li>').text(cat).appendTo(ul);
}

/ 13	. 

/ plugins

$ vi webpack.config.js

const webpack=require('webpack');									<-

module.exports={
	entry:'./src/app.js',
	output:{
		path:'./bin',
		filename:'app.bundle.js'
	},
	module:{
		loaders:[{
			test:/\.js$/,
			exclude:/node_modules/,
			loader:'babel-loader'
		}]
	},
	plugins:[
		new webpack.optimize.UglifyJsPlugin({
			compress:{	
				warnings:false
			},
			output:{
				comments:false
			}
		}),
	]
};

As of Babel 6.0.0 there are no plugins included by default. For babelify to be useful, you must also include some presets and/or plugins.

[eric@almond video]$ cat package.json

  "version": "1.0.0",
  "description": "",

  "scripts": {
    "start": "budo index.js --live"
  },
  "author": "",
  "license": "ISC",
  "devDependencies": {
    "babel": "^6.5.2",
    "babelify": "^7.2.0",
    "budo": "^8.1.0"
  },
  "browserify":{
	"transform":[[ "babelify", {"presets": ["es2015","react"]}]]
  }
}

	<Chat/>,
	document.getElementById('app')
);

$ vi index.js

var React=require('react');
var ReactDOM=require('react-dom');
var Chat=React.createClass({
  submit:function(ev){			
    ev.preventDefault();																				<-
  },
  render:function(){
    return <div>
      <div>Messages should displayed here</div>
      <form onSubmit={this.submit}>															<-
        <input type="text" placeholder="Your message..."/>
        <input type="submit" value="Send"/>
      </form>
    </div>
  }
});
ReactDOM.render(
  <Chat/>,
  document.getElementById('app')
);

/ Default wordt als we een form submit	, de index.html en bundle.js opnieuw reload	, en er wordt een nieuw screen create,
/ Dit is als er staat <form>	,
/ Maar we kunnen dit veranderen	, we moeten bij beide <- 	, dus <form onSubmit={this.submit}> en ev.preventDefault() in de this.submit()	,

/ we moeten in JSX camelcase onSubmit, terwijl in HTML het onsubmit wordt	,
/ Als we JavaScript willen in JSX, moet dat tussen {}	, dus {this.submit()}

var React=require('react');
var ReactDOM=require('react-dom');
var Chat=React.createClass({
  submit:function(ev){        // controller ,
    ev.preventDefault();
  },
  updateInput:function(ev){
    var text=ev.target.value;
    alert(text);																	<-
  },
  render:function(){          // view ,
    return <div>
      <div>Messages should displayed here</div>
      <form onSubmit={this.submit}>
        <input onChange={this.updateInput} type="text" placeholder="Your message..."/>
        <input type="submit" value="Send"/>
      </form>
    </div>
  }
});
ReactDOM.render(
  <Chat/>,
  document.getElementById('app')
);

/ als we een char geven in de text input	, dan verschijnt er een alert	,

$ vi index.js

var React=require('react');
var ReactDOM=require('react-dom');
var Chat=React.createClass({
  getInitialState:function(){ // state
    return {
      text:'',
      messages:[]
    };
  },
  updateInput:function(ev){   // controller , als je een char in text input geeft ,
    this.setState({
      text:ev.target.value
    });

  },
  submit:function(ev){        // controller , als je submit ,
    ev.preventDefault();
    this.setState({
      messages:this.state.messages.concat([
        this.state.text
      ])
    });
  },
 	render:function(){          // view ,
    return <div>
      <div>{this.state.messages}</div>
      <form onSubmit={this.submit}>
        <input onChange={this.updateInput} type="text" placeholder="Your message..."/>
        <input type="submit" value="Send"/>
      </form>
    </div>
  }
});
ReactDOM.render(
  <Chat/>,
  document.getElementById('app')
);

/ de state bestaat uit text , messages	, 
/ text is de current message	, iedere keer als je een char geeft in de text input	, komt deze erbij	, 
/ messages zijn alle eerdere text's 	, 

/ 13	. 

/ we maken iedere message op een aparte line	,

[eric@almond blog]$ pwd
/home/eric/Devel/JavaScript/Node/React/blog

var React=require('react');
var ReactDOM=require('react-dom');
var Chat=React.createClass({
	getInitialState:function(){ // state
		return {
			text:'',
			messages:[]
		};
	},
	updateInput:function(ev){ 	// controller	, als je een char in text input geeft	,
		this.setState({
			text:ev.target.value
		});
		
	},
	submit:function(ev){				// controller	, als je submit	,
		ev.preventDefault();
		var newMessage=<ChatMessage message={this.state.text}/>;
		this.setState({
			messages:this.state.messages.concat([
				newMessage
			])
		});
	},
	render:function(){					// view	,
		return <div>
			<div>{this.state.messages}</div>
			<form onSubmit={this.submit}>	
				<input onChange={this.updateInput} type="text" placeholder="Your message..."/>
				<input type="submit" value="Send"/>
			</form>	
		</div>
	}
});
ReactDOM.render(
	<Chat/>,
	document.getElementById('app')
);
var ChatMessage=React.createClass({
	render:function(){
		return <p>{this.props.message}</p>;
	}
});

var React=require('react');
var ReactDOM=require('react-dom');
var HelloWorld=React.createClass({

	propTypes:{
		name:React.PropTypes.string,
		isperson:React.PropTypes.bool
	},
	render:function(){
		var message="World";
		if(this.props.isperson){
			message=(<Person name={this.props.name}/>);
		}
		return(
			<h1>Hello {message}</h1>
		);
	}
});
var Person=React.createClass({

	propTypes:{
		name:React.PropTypes.string
	},
	render:function(){
		return(
			<span>{this.props.name}</span>
		);
	}
});
ReactDOM.render(
	<HelloWorld isperson={true} name="Foo Bar"/>,
	document.getElementById('app')
);

var React=require('react');
var ReactDOM=require('react-dom');
var HelloWorld=React.createClass({
	getDefaultProps:function(){
		return{
			name:"Gee Hee"
		};
	},
	propTypes:{
		name:React.PropTypes.string,
		isperson:React.PropTypes.bool
	},
	getInitialState:function(){
		return{
			value:13
		};
	},
  componentDidMount:function(){
    this.setState({value:this.state.value+7});
  },
	render:function(){
		return(
			<div>
				<h1>Hello {this.props.isperson?<Person name={this.props.name}/>:"World"}</h1>
				{this.state.value}	
			</div>
		);
	}
});
var Person=React.createClass({
	getDefaultProps:function(){
		return{
			name:"Gee Hee"
		};
	},
	propTypes:{
		name:React.PropTypes.string
	},
	render:function(){
		return(
			<span>{this.props.name}</span>
		);
	}
});
ReactDOM.render(
	<HelloWorld isperson={true} name="Foo Bar"/>,
	document.getElementById('app')
);

$ vi index.js

var React=require('react');
var ReactDOM=require('react-dom');
var HelloWorld=React.createClass({
	getDefaultProps:function(){
		return{
			name:"Gee Hee"
		};
	},
	propTypes:{
		name:React.PropTypes.string,
		isperson:React.PropTypes.bool
	},
	getInitialState:function(){
		return{
			value:13
		};
	},
	componentDidMount:function(){
		this.setState({value:this.state.value+7});
	},
	_addByOne:function(){
		console.log("Foo");
		this.setState({value:this.state.value+1});
	},
	_hello:function(){
		return(
			<h1>Hello</h1>
		);
	},
	render:function(){
		var s=<Person name={this.props.name}/>;
		console.log(s);
		return(
			<div>
				{this._hello()}
				<h1>Hello {this.props.isperson?<Person name={this.props.name}/>:"World"}</h1>
				{this.state.value}	
				<button onClick={this._addByOne}>Add by 1</button>
			</div>
		);
	}
});
var Person=React.createClass({
	getDefaultProps:function(){
		return{
			name:"Gee Hee"
		};
	},
	propTypes:{
		name:React.PropTypes.string
	},
	render:function(){
		return(
			<span>{this.props.name}</span>
		);
	}
});
ReactDOM.render(
	<HelloWorld isperson={true} name="Foo Bar"/>,
	document.getElementById('app')
);

/ we maken _addByOne, _hello	,

/ Let op () in 	,
				{this._hello()}
				<button onClick={this._addByOne}>Add by 1</button>

/ Met () wordt de aut. fct called	, in de onClick handler wil je dat niet, je wilt alleen dat hij wordt called als je click	,

				{this.props.contacts3.map((contact)=>{

import React from 'react';
import Contact from './contact';
/*
class ContactList extends React.Component{
	render(){
		return(
			<ul>
				<li>Foo Bar 1234</li>	
			</ul>
		);
	}
}
*/
var ContactList =React.createClass({
	getInitialState:function(){
		return{search:'Foo Bar'}
	},
	render:function(){
		console.log(this.props.contacts3);
		return(
			<div>
				<ul>
					{this.props.contacts3.map((contact)=>{
						return <Contact contact4={contact} key={contact.id}/>
					})}
					{this.props.contacts3.map(function(contact){
						return <Contact contact4={contact} key={contact.id}/>
					})};
				</ul>
				<input type="text" value={this.state.search} onChange={this.updateSearch}/>
			</div>
		);
	},
	updateSearch:function(event){
		console.log(event.target.value);
		this.setState({search:event.target.value});
	}
});
export default ContactList;

		console.log(this.props.contacts3);
		let self=this;
		let filtered=this.props.contacts3.filter(function(contact){
			return contact.name.toLowerCase().indexOf(self.state.search.toLowerCase())!==-1;
		});
/*
		let filtered=this.props.contacts3.filter((contact)=>{
			return contact.name.indexOf(this.state.search)!==-1;
		});
*/
		return(
			<div>
				<input type="text" value={this.state.search} onChange={this.updateSearch}/>
				<ul>
					{filtered.map(function(contact){
						return <Contact contact4={contact} key={contact.id}/>
					})}
				</ul>
			</div>
		);
	},
	updateSearch:function(event){
		console.log(event.target.value);
		this.setState({search:event.target.value});
	}
});
export default ContactList;

$ vi contact4.js

import React from 'react';
var Contact=React.createClass({
	render:function(){
		return(
			<li>{this.props.contact4.name} {this.props.contact4.phone}</li>
		);
	}
});
export default Contact;

/ REACT MANUAL WEBPACK 

/ See WEBPACK	AGAIN, we moeten een index.html hebben met src bundle.js	, want webapp-web-server creates deze bundle.js	, 
/ in package.json is de webpack-web-server call	, en in deze hoeft bundle.js niet te staan	,

/ In de webpack-dev-server call MOET --module-bind 'js=babel-loader'	, 
/ we zien dat we bundle.js NIET	,

////////////////////
    webpack-dev-server index.js --module-bind 'js=babel-loader'

/ als we alleen webpack call, doen we

    webpack index.js bundle.js --module-bind 'js=babel-loader'

[eric@almond webpack]$ pwd

 "scripts": {
    "start": "webpack index.js bundle.js --module-bind 'js=babel-loader'" , 
    "start":"webpack-dev-server index.js --module-bind 'js=babel-loader'"
  },
  "author": "",
  "license": "ISC",
  "dependencies": {
    "babel-core": "^6.9.1",
    "babel-loader": "^6.2.4",

https://github.com/Daniel15/babel-standalone

import React from 'react';

var CommentBox=React.createClass({
  render:function(){ 
    return(
      <div className='commentBox'>
        Hello, world! I am a CommentBox
      </div>
    );
  }
});
ReactDOM.render(<CommentBox/>,document.getElementById('content'));

The <div> tags are not actual DOM nodes; they are instantiations of React div components. You can think of these as markers or pieces of data that React knows how to handle. React is safe. We are not generating HTML strings so XSS protection is the default.

/ Dus React maakt WH meteen DOM elements	, 
/ we geven inderdaad geen string	, we quote niet <div ...

import React from 'react';
import ReactDOM from 'react-dom';

var CommentBox=React.createClass({
	render:function(){
		return(
			<div className='commentBox'>
				<h1>Comments</h1>
				<CommentList data={this.props.data}/>
				<CommentForm/>
			</div>
		);
	}
});
var CommentList=React.createClass({
	render:function(){
		var commentNodes=this.props.data.map(function(comment){
			return(
				<Comment author={comment.author} key={comment.id}>
					{comment.text}
				</Comment>
			);
		});
		return(
			<div className='commentList'>
				{commentNodes}	
			</div>
		);
	}
});
var CommentForm=React.createClass({
	render:function(){
		return(
			<div className='commentForm'>
				Hello, world! I am a CommentForm
			</div>
		);
	}
});
var Comment=React.createClass({
	render:function(){
		return(
			<div className='comment'>
				<h2 className='commentAuthor'>
					{this.props.author}
				</h2>
				{this.props.children}
			</div>
		);
	}
});

var data=[
	{id:1,author:"Peter Hunt",text:"This is one comment"},
	{id:2,author:"Jordan Walke",text:"This is *another* comment"}
];

ReactDOM.render(<CommentBox data={data}/>,document.getElementById('content'));

$ vi src/main.js

import React from 'react';
import ReactDOM from 'react-dom';
import $ from 'jquery';											<-

var CommentBox=React.createClass({
	getInitialState(){
		return {data:[]}
	},
	render:function(){
		return(
			<div className='commentBox'>
				<h1>Comments</h1>
				<CommentList data={this.state.data}/>		<- WAS: this.props.data
				<CommentForm/>
			</div>
		);
	},
	componentDidMount(){
		$.ajax({
			url:this.props.url,
			dataType:'json',
			cache:false,
			success:function(data){	
				this.setState({data:data});
			}.bind(this),
			error:function(xhr,status,err){
				console.error(this.props.url,status,err.toString());
			}.bind(this)
		});	
	},
});
var CommentList=React.createClass({
	render:function(){
		var commentNodes=this.props.data.map(function(comment){
			return(
				<Comment author={comment.author} key={comment.id}>
					{comment.text}
				</Comment>
			);
		});
		return(
			<div className='commentList'>
				{commentNodes}	
			</div>
		);
	}
});
var CommentForm=React.createClass({
	render:function(){
		return(
			<div className='commentForm'>
				Hello, world! I am a CommentForm
			</div>
		);
	}
});
var Comment=React.createClass({
	render:function(){
		return(
			<div className='comment'>
				<h2 className='commentAuthor'>
					{this.props.author}
				</h2>
				{this.props.children}
			</div>
		);
	}
});

ReactDOM.render(
	<CommentBox url='/comments'/>,				<- WAS: data={data}	, en dan werd this.props.data	
																								used in CommentBox	,

	res.json(obj);
});

	fs.readFile('./data.json','utf-8',function(err,data){
		var obj=JSON.parse(data);
		res.json(obj);
	});
});

/ De submit handler van het CommentForm calls fct in CommentBox, die de state van de CommentBox set	, want daar is de state	, en via props, gaat deze state de CommentList in	, in CommentBox's render fct 	,
	<CommentList data={this.state.data} />
/ en CommentList doet	,
    var commentNodes=this.props.data.map(function(comment){

$ vi src/main.js

import React from 'react';
import ReactDOM from 'react-dom';
import $ from 'jquery';

var CommentBox=React.createClass({
	getInitialState:function(){
		return {data:[]}
	},
	loadCommentsFromServer:function(){
		$.ajax({
			url:this.props.url,
			dataType:'json',
			cache:false,															<- TODO
			success:function(data){	
				this.setState({data:data});
			}.bind(this),
			error:function(xhr,status,err){
				console.error(this.props.url,status,err.toString());
			}.bind(this)
		});	
	},
	componentDidMount:function(){
		this.loadCommentsFromServer();
		setInterval(this.loadCommentsFromServer,this.props.pollInterval);
	},
	handleCommentSubmit:function(comment){
		$.ajax({
			url:this.props.url,
			dataType:'json',
			type:'POST',
			contentType:'application/json;charset=utf-8',			<-
			data:JSON.stringify(comment),											<-
			success:function(data){	
				this.setState({data:data});
			}.bind(this),
			error:function(xhr,status,err){
				console.error(this.props.url,status,err.toString());
			}.bind(this)
		});	
	},
	render:function(){
		return(
			<div className='commentBox'>
				<h1>Comments</h1>
				<CommentList data={this.state.data}/>
				<CommentForm onCommentSubmit={this.handleCommentSubmit}/>
			</div>
		);
	},
});
var CommentList=React.createClass({
	render:function(){
		var commentNodes=this.props.data.map(function(comment){
			return(
				<Comment author={comment.author} key={comment.id}>
					{comment.text}
				</Comment>
			);
		});
		return(
			<div className='commentList'>
				{commentNodes}	
			</div>
		);
	}
});
var CommentForm=React.createClass({
	getInitialState:function(){
		return{
			author:'',
			text:''
		};
	},
	handleAuthorChange:function(e){
		this.setState({author:e.target.value});
	},
	handleTextChange:function(e){
		this.setState({text:e.target.value});
	},
	handleSubmit:function(e){
		e.preventDefault();
		var author=this.state.author.trim();
		var text=this.state.text.trim();	
		if(!author || !text){
			return;
		}
		this.props.onCommentSubmit({author:author,text:text});
		this.setState({author:'',text:''});
	
	},
	
	render:function(){
		return(
			<form className='commentForm' onSubmit={this.handleSubmit}>
				<input 
					type='text' 
					placeHolder='Your name...'
					value={this.state.author}
					onChange={this.handleAuthorChange}
				/>																				<- />
				<input 
					type='text' 
					placeHolder='Your name...'
					value={this.state.text}
					onChange={this.handleTextChange}
				/>
				<input type='submit' value='Post'/>
			</form>
		);
	}
});
var Comment=React.createClass({
	render:function(){
		return(
			<div className='comment'>
				<h2 className='commentAuthor'>
					{this.props.author}
				</h2>
				{this.props.children}
			</div>
		);
	}
});

ReactDOM.render(
	<CommentBox url='/comments' pollInterval={10000}/>
	,document.getElementById('content'));

$ vi server.js

var express=require('express');
var server=express();
server.use(express.static('public'));
server.use('/static',express.static('bin'));
server.listen(3000);

var fs=require('fs');
/*
server.get('/comments',function(req,res){
	var data=fs.readFileSync('./data.json','utf-8');
	var obj=JSON.parse(data);
	res.json(obj);
});
*/
server.get('/comments',function(req,res){
	fs.readFile('./data.json','utf-8',function(err,data){
		var arr=JSON.parse(data);
		res.json(arr);
	});
});

var bodyParser=require('body-parser');
//var parseUrlEncoded=bodyParser.urlencoded({extended:false});
var jsonParser=bodyParser.json();
var id=3;
//server.post('/comments',parseUrlEncoded,function(req,res){
server.post('/comments',jsonParser,function(req,res){
	req.body.id=id++;
	fs.readFile('./data.json','utf-8',function(err,data){
		var arr=JSON.parse(data);
		arr.push(req.body);
		var str=JSON.stringify(arr)
		fs.writeFile('./data.json',str,'utf-8',function(err){
			if(err)throw err;
			console.log('Wrote data');
		});
	});
});

/ Set antwoord alvast op het scherm	,

var CommentBox=React.createClass({
 	handleCommentSubmit:function(comment){
    var comments=this.state.data;														<-
    comment.id=Date.now();																	<-
    var newComments=comments.concat([comment]);							<-
    this.setState({data:newComments});											<-
    $.ajax({																								<- onveranderd	,
      url:this.props.url,
      dataType:'json',
      type:'POST',
      contentType:'application/json;charset=utf-8',
      data:JSON.stringify(comment),
      success:function(data){
        this.setState({data:data});
      }.bind(this),
      error:function(xhr,status,err){
        this.setState({data:comments});
        console.error(this.props.url,status,err.toString());
      }.bind(this)
    });
  },

var webpack=require('webpack');
module.exports={
	entry:'./src/main.js',
	output:{
		path:'./bin',
		filename:'app.bundle.js'
	},
	module:{
		loaders:[{
			test:/\.js$/,
			include:/src/,
			loader:'babel-loader'
		},{
			test:/\.css$/,
			include:/src/,
			loader:'style!css'
		},
    { test: /\.woff(\?v=\d+\.\d+\.\d+)?$/,   
			loader: "url?limit=10000&minetype=application/font-woff" },
    { test: /\.ttf(\?v=\d+\.\d+\.\d+)?$/,    
			loader: "url?limit=10000&minetype=application/octet-stream" },
    { test: /\.eot(\?v=\d+\.\d+\.\d+)?$/,    
			loader: "file" },
    { test: /\.svg(\?v=\d+\.\d+\.\d+)?$/,    
			loader: "url?limit=10000&minetype=image/svg+xml" },
    { test: /\.woff2(\?v=\d+\.\d+\.\d+)?$/,   
			loader: "url?limit=10000&minetype=application/font-woff2" }
		]
	},
}

/ video 2.9

/ Als we de browser smal maken, komen de .col-md-4 columns onder elkaar	. Hoe fix?

/ we used .col-md-* 	, md= medium	, dat is laptop	, voor 992px+ screen sizes	,

/ Smal: .col-sm-*	, .col-sm-offset-*, 768px+	,

/ .col-sm-4 takes 4 columns for small and medium sized devices	,

/ md: laptop	, 992px+
/ sm: tablet	, 768px+ 
/ xs: phone	,	0px+

/ 13	. 

/we veranderen .col-md-4 in .col-sm-4	, 
/ we zien dat als het de browser smaller maken, de 3 columns naast elkaar blijven	, 
/ maar als we de browser heel smal maken, komen ze toch weer onder elkaar	,

/ we maken de 3 column .col-xs-4	,
/ voor md, ms, and xs	,

/ als we HTML veranderen, hoeven we alleen F5 te doen	, server restart is niet nodig	,

/ 1313	. 

/ Deze doet het OK in md, sm, xs	,

/ video 4.8

/ we halen de navigation uit de grid	, dus uit .container	,
/ .container gaf margins links en rechts, en centered de page	, 
/ de navigation bar stretches over the whole page	,

/ Haal de grid eruit	,
/ we willen de width van de navigation bar determined by its content, not by the grid system	,

/ Ook set we de navigation in aparte <div class="container"></div>	, anders valt hij in grijze gebied met buttons	, 
/ TODO

/ WAS	,
    <div class='container'>

      <div class='row'>
        <div class='col-md-12'>
          <h1>Blasting off with Bootstrap</h1>
        </div>
      </div>
			...

/ NU	,
    <div class='container'>
          <h1>Blasting off with Bootstrap</h1>
		</div>
    <div class='container'>

/ we willen de <h1/> be a link to our home page	,

       <a href='/' class='navbar-brand'>Blasting off with Bootstrap</a>

/ .navbar-brand: stands out,	 is to the left of the page	,
/ je kunt ook je company logo hier set	,

/ we kunnen 	, 
.nav .nav-pills			: appear horizontally
.nav .nav-tabs			:	appear horizontally, content below belongs to the tab	,
.nav .navbar-nav		: like .nav-pills	, but without rounded borders	,
	
/ we doen	,
.nav .navbar-nav .navbar-right

   <div class='container'>

/ 13	.

/ data-toggle='dropdown'

/ als we page open, is sub menu niet zichtbaar	, als we click op About, wordt sub menu zichtbaar, en als we weer click op About, verdwijnt hij weer	, 

/ Ook in xs werkt OK	,

/ Als we click op About, bootstrap add class .open aan parent <li/> , en als bootstrap li.open elem sees	, met een child ul.dropdown-menu, dan shows bootstrap  deze ul	,

        <ul class="nav navbar-nav navbar-right collapse navbar-collapse">
          <li><a href="index.html">Home</a></li>
          <li><a href="tickets.html">Tickets</a></li>
          <li>
            <a href="#" data-toggle='dropdown'>About <span class='caret'></span></a>					<-
            <ul class='dropdown-menu'>
              <li><a href='story.html'>Our Story</a></li> 
              <li><a href='contact.html'>Contact Us</a></li>  
              <li><a href='/blog'>Blog</a></li> 
              <li><a href='http://twitter.com'>Twitter</a></li> 
              <li><a href='http://facebook.com'>Facebook</a></li> 
            </ul>
          </li>
        </ul>

import React from 'react';
import ReactDOM from 'react-dom';

var StoryBox=React.createClass({
	render:function(){
		const now=new Date();
		const topics=['HTML','JavaScript','React'];
		return (
			<div>	
				<div className='navbar navbar-default navbar-static-top'>
					<div className='container'>
						<div className='navbar-header'>
							<a href='/' className='navbar-brand'>Stories</a>
						</div>
					</div>
				</div>
				<div className='container'>
					<div className='row well well-lg'>
						<div className='col-xs-6'>
							<p className='lead'>Current time:{now.toTimeString()}</p>
						</div>
						<ul className='col-xs-6 list-unstyled'>
							{topics.map(topic=><li>{topic}</li>)}
						</ul>
					</div>	
				</div>
			</div>
		);
	}
});
ReactDOM.render(<StoryBox/>,document.getElementById('content'));

import React from 'react';
import ReactDOM from 'react-dom';

var CommentBox=React.createClass({
	render:function(){
		return(
			<div className='container'>
				<h3>Comments</h3>
				<h4>2 comments</h4>
				<ul className='list-group'>
					<li className='list-group-item'>
						<Comment author='Foo Bar' body='Interesting...'/>
					</li>
					<li className='list-group-item'>
						<Comment author='π ε' body='My Greek letters...'/>
					</li>
				</ul>
			</div>
		);
	}
});
var Comment=React.createClass({
	render:function(){
		return(
			<div>
				<p>{this.props.author}</p>
				<p>{this.props.body}</p>
				<div>
					<a href='#'>Delete comment</a>
				</div>
			</div>
		);
	}
});

ReactDOM.render(<CommentBox/>,document.getElementById('content'));

/ video 2.4

import React from 'react';
import ReactDOM from 'react-dom';

var CommentBox=React.createClass({
	render:function(){
		const comments=[
			{id:1,author:'Foo Bar',body:'Interesting...'},
			{id:2,author:'π ε',body:'My Greek letters...'}
		];
		return(
			<div className='container'>
				<h3>Comments</h3>
				<h4>{comments.length} comments</h4>
				<ul className='list-group'>
					{comments.map(comment=>
						<li key={comment.id} className='list-group-item'>						<- key attr moet op li	, niet op Comment
							<Comment author={comment.author} body={comment.body}/>
						</li>
					)}
				</ul>
			</div>
		);
	}
});
var Comment=React.createClass({
	render:function(){
		return(
			<div>
				<p>{this.props.author}</p>
				<p>{this.props.body}</p>
				<div>
					<a href='#'>Delete comment</a>
				</div>
			</div>
		);
	}
});

ReactDOM.render(<CommentBox/>,document.getElementById('content'));

import React from 'react';
import ReactDOM from 'react-dom';

var CommentBox=React.createClass({
	getInitialState:function(){
		return {showComments:true}
	},
	render:function(){
		const comments=[
			{id:1,author:'Foo Bar',body:'Interesting...'},
			{id:2,author:'π ε',body:'My Greek letters...'}
		];
		return(
			<div className='container'>
				<h3>Comments</h3>
				<h4>{comments.length} comments</h4>
				{if(this.state.showComments){																			<-
					return(
						<ul className='list-group'>
							{comments.map(comment=>
								<li key={comment.id} className='list-group-item'>
									<Comment author={comment.author} body={comment.body}/>
								</li>
							)}
						</ul>
					);
				}}
			</div>
		);
	}
});
var Comment=React.createClass({
	render:function(){
		return(
			<div>
				<p>{this.props.author}</p>
				<p>{this.props.body}</p>
				<div>
					<a href='#'>Delete comment</a>
				</div>
			</div>
		);
	}
});

ReactDOM.render(<CommentBox/>,document.getElementById('content'));

import React from 'react';
import ReactDOM from 'react-dom';

var CommentBox=React.createClass({
	getInitialState:function(){
		return {showComments:true}
	},
	_renderList(){
		if(this.state.showComments){
			return(
				<ul className='list-group'>
					{this._getComments().map(comment=>
						<li key={comment.id} className='list-group-item'>
							<Comment author={comment.author} body={comment.body}/>
						</li>
					)}
				</ul>
			);
		}
	},
	_getComments(){
		return [
			{id:1,author:'Foo Bar',body:'Interesting...'},
			{id:2,author:'π ε',body:'My Greek letters...'}
		];
	},
	render:function(){
		const comments=[
			{id:1,author:'Foo Bar',body:'Interesting...'},
			{id:2,author:'π ε',body:'My Greek letters...'}
		];
		return(
			<div className='container'>
				<h3>Comments</h3>
				<h4>{comments.length} comments</h4>
				{this._renderList()}
			</div>
		);
	}
});

      if(this.state.showComments){
			...
		}
	}.bind(this)()

/ we moeten bind(this)	, anders is this in de immediately executing function undefined	, en kan this.state NIET	,

import React from 'react';
import ReactDOM from 'react-dom';

var CommentBox=React.createClass({
	getInitialState:function(){
		return {showComments:false}
	},
	_handleClick:function(){
		this.setState({showComments:!this.state.showComments});
	},
	render:function(){
		const comments=[
			{id:1,author:'Foo Bar',body:'Interesting...'},
			{id:2,author:'π ε',body:'My Greek letters...'}
		];
		return(
			<div className='container'>
				<h3>Comments</h3>
				<button onClick={this._handleClick}>Show</button>									<-
				<h4>{comments.length} comments</h4>
				{(function(){
					if(this.state.showComments){
						return(
							<ul className='list-group'>
								{comments.map(comment=>
									<li key={comment.id} className='list-group-item'>
										<Comment author={comment.author} body={comment.body}/>
									</li>
								)}
							</ul>
						);
					}
				}).bind(this)()}

			</div>
		);
	}
});

		return(

		);
	}
});

$ vi src/main.js

import React from 'react';
import ReactDOM from 'react-dom';

var CommentBox=React.createClass({
	getInitialState:function(){
		return {showComments:false}
	},
	_handleClick:function(){
		this.setState({showComments:!this.state.showComments});
	},
	render:function(){
		const comments=[
			{id:1,author:'Foo Bar',body:'Interesting...'},
			{id:2,author:'π ε',body:'My Greek letters...'}
		];
		return(
			<div className='container'>
				<div className='row'> 
					<h3>Comments</h3>
				</div>
				<div className='row well well-lg'> 
					<div className='col-xs-6'>
						<button 
							onClick={
								(function(){
									this.setState({showComments:!this.state.showComments})
								}).bind(this)
							} 
							className='btn btn-primary'>{
								(function(){
									if(this.state.showComments){
										return 'Hide comments'
									}else{
										return 'Show comments'
									}
								}).bind(this)()
							}
						</button>
					</div>
				</div>
				<div className='row'> 
					<div className='col-xs-6'>
						<h4>{comments.length} comments</h4>
					</div>
				</div>
				<div className='row'> 
					<div className='col-xs-6'>{
						(function(){
							if(this.state.showComments){
								return(
									<ul className='list-group'>
										{comments.map(comment=>
											<li key={comment.id} className='list-group-item'>
												<Comment author={comment.author} body={comment.body}/>
											</li>
										)}
									</ul>
								);
							}
						}).bind(this)()
					}
					</div>
				</div>
			</div>
		);
	}
});
var Comment=React.createClass({
	render:function(){
		return(
			<div>
				<p>{this.props.author}</p>
				<p>{this.props.body}</p>
				<div>
					<a href='#'>Delete comment</a>
				</div>
			</div>
		);
	}
});

ReactDOM.render(<CommentBox/>,document.getElementById('content'));

$ vi src/main.js

import React from 'react';
import ReactDOM from 'react-dom';

var CommentBox=React.createClass({
	getInitialState:function(){
		return {
			showComments:true,
			comments:[]
		}
	},
	componentDidMount:function(){
		this.setState({
			comments:this.state.comments.concat([
				{id:1,name:'Foo Bar',text:'Interesting...'},
				{id:2,name:'π ε',text:'My Greek letters...'}
			])
		});
	},
	_handleClick:function(){
		this.setState({showComments:!this.state.showComments});
	},
	_handleCommentSubmit(comment){
		comment.id=this.state.comments.length+1;
		//this.state.comments.push(comment);															<- OK					
		//this.setState({comments:this.state.comments});									<- OK, 
		// or	,
		this.setState({comments:this.state.comments.concat([comment])});	<- OK	,
	},
	render:function(){
		return(
			<div className='container'>
				<div className='row'> 
					<h3>Comments</h3>
				</div>
				<CommentForm onCommentSubmit={this._handleCommentSubmit}/>
				<div className='row'> 
					<div className='col-xs-6'>
						<button 
							onClick={
								(function(){
									this.setState({showComments:!this.state.showComments})
								}).bind(this)
							} 
							className='btn btn-default'>{
								(function(){
									if(this.state.showComments){
										return 'Hide comments'
									}else{
										return 'Show comments'
									}
								}).bind(this)()
							}
						</button>
					</div>
				</div>
				<div className='row'> 
					<div className='col-xs-6'>
						<h4>{this.state.comments.length} comments</h4>
					</div>
				</div>
				<div className='row'> 
					<div className='col-xs-6'>{
						(function(){
							if(this.state.showComments){
								return(
									<ul className='list-group'>
										{this.state.comments.map(comment=>
											<li key={comment.id} className='list-group-item'>
												<Comment key={comment.id} name={comment.name} text={comment.text}/>
											</li>
										)}
									</ul>
								);
							}
						}).bind(this)()
					}
					</div>
				</div>
			</div>
		);
	}
});
var Comment=React.createClass({
	render:function(){
		return(
			<div>
				<p>{this.props.name}</p>
				<p>{this.props.text}</p>
				<div>
					<a href='#'>Delete comment</a>
				</div>
			</div>
		);
	}
});
var CommentForm=React.createClass({
	getInitialState(){
		return {name:'',text:''}
	},
	_handleNameChange:function(e){
		this.setState({name:e.target.value});
	},
	_handleTextChange:function(e){
		this.setState({text:e.target.value});
	},
	_handleSubmit:function(e){
		e.preventDefault();	
		var name=this.state.name.trim();
		var text=this.state.text.trim();
		if(!name || !text)return;
		this.props.onCommentSubmit({name:name,text:text});
		this.setState({name:'',text:''});
	},
	render:function(){
		return(
			<div className='row well well-lg'>
					<form className='form-horizontal' onSubmit={this._handleSubmit}>
						<div className='form-group'>
							<label htmlFor='name' className='col-xs-2 control-label'>Name</label>
							<div className='col-xs-10'>
								<input
									className='form-control'
									id='name'
									type='text'
									placeholder='Your name...'
									value={this.state.name}
									onChange={this._handleNameChange}/>
							</div>	
						</div>
						<div className='form-group'>
							<label htmlFor='text' className='col-xs-2 control-label'>Text</label>
							<div className='col-xs-10'>
								<textarea
									className='form-control'
									id='text'
									placeholder='Your text...'
									value={this.state.text}
									onChange={this._handleTextChange}/>
							</div>	
						</div>
						<div className='form-group'>
							<div className='col-xs-offset-2 col-xs-8'>	
								<button className='btn btn-primary'>Post</button>
							</div>
						</div>
					</form>
				</div>
		);
	}
});

ReactDOM.render(<CommentBox/>,document.getElementById('content'));

$ vi src/main.js

import React from 'react';
import ReactDOM from 'react-dom';
import $ from 'jquery';

var CommentBox=React.createClass({
	getInitialState:function(){
		return {data:[]}
	},
	loadCommentsFromServer:function(){
		$.ajax({
			url:this.props.url,
			dataType:'json',
			cache:false,
			success:function(data){	
				this.setState({data:data});
			}.bind(this),
			error:function(xhr,status,err){
				console.error(this.props.url,status,err.toString());
			}.bind(this)
		});	
	},
	componentDidMount:function(){
		this.loadCommentsFromServer();
		setInterval(this.loadCommentsFromServer,this.props.pollInterval);
	},
	handleCommentSubmit:function(comment){
		var comments=this.state.data;
		comment.id=Date.now();
		var newComments=comments.concat([comment]);
		this.setState({data:newComments});
		$.ajax({
			url:this.props.url,
			dataType:'json',
			type:'POST',
			contentType:'application/json;charset=utf-8',
			data:JSON.stringify(comment),
			success:function(data){	
				this.setState({data:data});
			}.bind(this),
			error:function(xhr,status,err){
				this.setState({data:comments});
				console.error(this.props.url,status,err.toString());
			}.bind(this)
		});	
	},
	render:function(){
		return(
			<div className='commentBox container'>														<-
				<div className='row'>																						<-
					<h1>Comments</h1>
				</div>
				<div className='row well well-lg'>															<-
					<CommentForm onCommentSubmit={this.handleCommentSubmit}/>
				</div>
				<div className='row'>																						<-
					<CommentList data={this.state.data}/>
				</div>
			</div>
		);
	},
});
var CommentList=React.createClass({
	render:function(){
		var commentNodes=this.props.data.map(function(comment){
			return(
				<li className='list-group-item'>																<-
					<Comment author={comment.author} key={comment.id}>
						{comment.text}
					</Comment>
				</li>
			);
		});
		return(
			<ul className='list-group'>																				<-
				{commentNodes}
			</ul>
		);
	}
});
var CommentForm=React.createClass({
	getInitialState:function(){
		return{
			author:'',
			text:''
		};
	},
	handleAuthorChange:function(e){
		this.setState({author:e.target.value});
	},
	handleTextChange:function(e){
		this.setState({text:e.target.value});
	},
	handleSubmit:function(e){
		e.preventDefault();
		var author=this.state.author.trim();
		var text=this.state.text.trim();	
		if(!author || !text){
			return;
		}
		this.props.onCommentSubmit({author:author,text:text});
		this.setState({author:'',text:''});
	
	},
	
	render:function(){
		return(
			<form className='form-horizontal' onSubmit={this.handleSubmit}>									<-
				<div className='form-group'>																									<-
					<label for='author' className='col-sm-2 control-label'>Author</label>				<-
					<div className='col-sm-10'>																									<-
						<input 
							className='form-control'																								<-
							id='author'																															<-
							type='text' 
							placeholder='Your name...'
							value={this.state.author}
							onChange={this.handleAuthorChange}/>
					</div>
				</div>
				<div className='form-group'>																									<-
					<label for='text' className='col-sm-2 control-label'>Text</label>						<-
					<div className='col-sm-10'>																									<-
						<input 
							className='form-control'																								<-
							id='text'																																<-
							type='text' 
							placeholder='Your text...'
							value={this.state.text}
							onChange={this.handleTextChange}/>
					</div>
				</div>
				<div className='form-group'>																									<-
					<div className='col-sm-offset-2 col-sm-10'>																	<-
						<button 																																	<-
							type="submit" 																													<-
							className='btn btn-primary'>Post																				<-
						</button>
					</div>
				</div>
			</form>
		);
	}
});
var Comment=React.createClass({
	render:function(){
		return(
			<div className='comment'>
				<h2 className='commentAuthor'>
					{this.props.author}
				</h2>
				{this.props.children}
			</div>
		);
	}
});

ReactDOM.render(
	<CommentBox url='/comments' pollInterval={10000}/>
	,document.getElementById('content'));

/ Lees 
https://facebook.github.io/react/docs/tutorial.html

With the traditional DOM, input elements are rendered and the browser manages the state (its rendered value). As a result, the state of the actual DOM will differ from that of the component. This is not ideal as the state of the view will differ from that of the component. In React, components should always represent the state of the view and not only at the point of initialization.

/ Klopt	, met service side frameworks is naast de DOM component er een component op de server	, waar de state in is	,
/ Met angular, react is die component er client side	,
/ Met angular1 bijv	, 
<div ng-controller="ExampleController">
  <form novalidate class="simple-form">
    Name: <input type="text" ng-model="user.name" /><br />
    E-mail: <input type="email" ng-model="user.email" /><br />
    Gender: <input type="radio" ng-model="user.gender" value="male" />male
    <input type="radio" ng-model="user.gender" value="female" />female<br />
    <input type="button" ng-click="reset()" value="Reset" />
    <input type="submit" ng-click="update(user)" value="Save" />
  </form>
  <pre>user = {{user | json}}</pre>
  <pre>master = {{master | json}}</pre>
</div>

<script>
  angular.module('formExample', [])
    .controller('ExampleController', ['$scope', function($scope) {
      $scope.master = {};

      $scope.update = function(user) {
        $scope.master = angular.copy(user);
      };

/ in scope is user	, deze maakt angular, omdat we ng-model='user.name' write	,

[eric@almond express_]$ cat src/main.js 
import $ from 'jquery';
$('form').on('submit',function(event){
	event.preventDefault();
	var form=$(this);
	var data=form.serialize();
	$.ajax({
		type:'POST',
		url:'/my',
    contentType:'application/x-www-form-urlencoded',
		data:data
	}).done(function(data){
		for(var key in data){
			var html=$.parseHTML(data[key],document,true);
			for(var i in html){
				$('body').append(html[i]);
			}
			//$('body').append(data[key]);									<- (**)
			//var script=$(data[key])[0];
			//document.body.appendChild(script);
			//document.body.innerHTML=data[key];
		}
		form.trigger('reset');
	});
})

$ npm i jquery --save

$ vi index.js

var React=require('react');
var ReactDOM=require('react-dom');
var CommentList=require('./tutorial2');
var CommentForm=require('./tutorial3');
var $=require('jquery');

var CommentBox=React.createClass({
	getInitialState:function(){
		return {
			data:[]
		}
	},
	componentDidMount:function(){
		$.ajax({
			url:this.props.url,
			dataType:"json",
			cache:false,
			success:function(data){
				this.setState({data:data});
			}.bind(this),
			error:function(xhr,status,err){
				console.error(this.props.url,status,err.toString());
			}.bind(this)
		});	
	},
	render:function(){
		return(
			<div className="commentBox">
				<h1>Comments</h1>
				<CommentList data={this.state.data}/>
				<CommentForm/>
			</div>
		);
	}	
});
ReactDOM.render(
 	<CommentBox url="comments.json"/>,	
	document.getElementById('example')
);

/ De url is relative , tegen localhost:8080	, 
/ we kunnen ook in de browser localhost:8080/comments.json geven	, 

/ comments.json is niet client side, in de browser	, alleen op de server	, 
/ webpack-dev-server is een server	,

/ Als we een b set in ComponentDidMount,	 dan zien we inderdaad	, dat de page er al is	, alleen nog geen data in <div class="commentList"></div>

/ componentDidMount calls .setState in de success fct	, daardoor wordt de view updated	,  dit gebeurt in de browser	,

/ 7	. 

/ we poll elke 2s	, 
/ Inderdaad	, als we comments.json edit	, zie je dat in de browser	,

$ vi index.js

var React=require('react');
var ReactDOM=require('react-dom');
var CommentList=require('./tutorial2');
var CommentForm=require('./tutorial3');
var $=require('jquery');

var CommentBox=React.createClass({
	getInitialState:function(){
		return {
			data:[]
		}
	},
	loadCommentsFromServer:function(){
		$.ajax({
			url:this.props.url,
			dataType:"json",
			cache:false,
			success:function(data){
				this.setState({data:data});
			}.bind(this),
			error:function(xhr,status,err){
				console.error(this.props.url,status,err.toString());
			}.bind(this)
		});	
	},
	componentDidMount:function(){
		this.loadCommentsFromServer();
		setInterval(this.loadCommentsFromServer,this.props.pollInterval);
		
	},
	render:function(){
		return(
			<div className="commentBox">
				<h1>Comments</h1>
				<CommentList data={this.state.data}/>
				<CommentForm/>
			</div>
		);
	}	
});
ReactDOM.render(
 	<CommentBox url="comments.json" pollInterval={2000}/>,	
	document.getElementById('example')
);

/ 7	. 

$ vi tutorial3.js

var React=require('react');

var CommentForm=React.createClass({
	render:function(){
		return(
			<form className="commentForm">
				<input type="text" placeHolder="Your name..."/>
				<input type="text" placeHolder="Say something..."/>
				<input type="submit" value="Post"/>
			</form>
		);
	}
});
module.exports=CommentForm;

/ <input> is hier een DOM elem, de state wordt managed door de browser	, 
/ Als we iets geven, dan is deze state != state van de component, die ook in de browser is	,  

This is not ideal as the state of the view will differ from that of the component. In React, components should always represent the state of the view and not only at the point of initialization. 	 
/ Dat laatste is inderdaad zo: bij init zien we de state van de component , maar als we edit,	 worden ze ongelijk	,

/ we set de poll even uit	,
$ vi index.js
  <CommentBox url="comments.json" pollInterval={24*60*60*1000}/>,

$ vi tutorial3.js

var React=require('react');

var CommentForm=React.createClass({
	getInitialState:function(){
		return {
			author:"",
			text:""
		};
	},
	handleAuthorChange:function(event){
		this.setState({author:event.target.value});
	},
	handleTextChange:function(event){
		this.setState({text:event.target.value});
	},
	handleSubmit:function(event){
		event.preventDefault();
		var author=this.state.author.trim();
		var text=this.state.text.trim();
		if(!text || !author){
			return;
		}
	//	this.setState({author:"",text:""});
	},
	render:function(){
		return(
			<form className="commentForm" onSubmit={this.handleSubmit}>
				<input 
					type="text" 
					placeHolder="Your name..."
					value={this.state.author}
					onChange={this.handleAuthorChange}		
				/>
				<input 
					type="text" 
					placeHolder="Say something..."
					value={this.state.text}
					onChange={this.handleTextChange}		
				/>
				<input type="submit" value="Post"/>
			</form>
		);
	}
});
module.exports=CommentForm;


/ 13	. 

	handleAuthorChange:function(event){
		this.setState({author:event.target.value});
	},
/ Als we .setState NIET 	, dan zien de char niet in de input	, dus de UI wordt niet update	, omdat .setState niet wordt called	,
/ Als we achter .setState this.state bekijken, zien we de huidige state, dus zonder het char wat we gaven	, this.setState queues	, en de char moet nog worden processed	,
/ Dit heeft allemaal niets te maken met de submit	,

/ 7	. 

/ we hebben hieronder een POST gemaakt	, maar we kunnen NIET	post naar comments.json	, alleen GET,
Cannot POST /comments.json
/ Dus de POST hieronder werkt NIET	, 

$ vi index.js

var React=require('react');
var ReactDOM=require('react-dom');
var CommentList=require('./tutorial2');
var CommentForm=require('./tutorial3');
var $=require('jquery');

var CommentBox=React.createClass({
	getInitialState:function(){
		return {
			data:[]
		}
	},
	loadCommentsFromServer:function(){
		$.ajax({
			url:this.props.url,
			dataType:"json",
			cache:false,
			success:function(data){
				this.setState({data:data});
			}.bind(this),
			error:function(xhr,status,err){
				console.error(this.props.url,status,err.toString());
			}.bind(this)
		});	
	},
	componentDidMount:function(){
		this.loadCommentsFromServer();
		setInterval(this.loadCommentsFromServer,this.props.pollInterval);
		
	},
	handleCommentSubmit:function(comment){	
		$.ajax({
			url:this.props.url,
			dataType:"json",
			type:"POST",
			data:comment,
			success:function(data){
				this.setState({data:data});
			}.bind(this),
			error:function(xhr,status,err){
				console.error(this.props.url,status,err.toString());
			}.bind(this)
		});	

	},
	render:function(){
		return(
			<div className="commentBox">
				<h1>Comments</h1>
				<CommentList data={this.state.data}/>
				<CommentForm onCommentSubmit={this.handleCommentSubmit}/>
			</div>
		);
	}	
});
ReactDOM.render(
 	<CommentBox url="comments.json" pollInterval={24*60*60*1000}/>,	
	document.getElementById('example')
);

$ vi tutorial3.js

var React=require('react');

var CommentForm=React.createClass({
	getInitialState:function(){
		return {
			author:"",
			text:""
		};
	},
	handleAuthorChange:function(event){
		this.setState({author:event.target.value});
	},
	handleTextChange:function(event){
		this.setState({text:event.target.value});
	},
	handleSubmit:function(event){
		event.preventDefault();
		var author=this.state.author.trim();
		var text=this.state.text.trim();
		if(!text || !author){
			return;
		}
		this.props.onCommentSubmit({author:author,text:text});			// <-
		this.setState({author:"",text:""});
	},
	render:function(){
		return(
			<form className="commentForm" onSubmit={this.handleSubmit}>
				<input 
					type="text" 
					placeHolder="Your name..."
					value={this.state.author}
					onChange={this.handleAuthorChange}		
				/>
				<input 
					type="text" 
					placeHolder="Say something..."
					value={this.state.text}
					onChange={this.handleTextChange}		
				/>
				<input type="submit" value="Post"/>
			</form>
		);
	}
});
module.exports=CommentForm;

/ level 1

/ create simple web api server	, which accepts http request on the root path	, and responses with a string "Hello, world!"

$ vi index.js

var express=require('express');
var app=express();
app.get("/",function(req,res){
	res.send("Hello, world!");
});
app.listen(3000,function(){
	console.log("Listening on tcp port 3000...");
});

/ server.js serves HTML	, en hoe met public/index.html

/ on the appl inst we can call functions which create routes	, the get fct creates routes which accepts GET reqs	, 
/ we give the get fct a path, "/",

/ Lees	,
https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/HTTP_302
/ http 1.0: 302 Moved Temporarily	. 
/ Nu ipv 302 zijn er 303, 307	, 303: redirect to GET	, 307: redirect to same	, 

/ 301	,

$ vi index.js

var express=require('express');
var app=express();

app.get("/",function(req,res){
  res.sendFile(__dirname+'/public/index.html');
});
// of	,
app.use(express.static('public'));

app.listen(3000);

/ static middleware	, default to serve the index.html in the folder which is the argument	, here 'public'	,
/ Als in index.html	, 
	<img src="gerbra.jpg">
/ vindt de static middleware deze ook	,
/ Maar defaults to index.html inderdaad	, daarna vervolgstappen zoals images	, die in index.html staan	,

///////////////////////////////
/ Als we app.use 	, dan dus GEEN route	,
app.use(express.static('public'));
/ of	,
app.use(function(req,res,next){
	res.send('Done!');
}

/ Intermezzo

/ we moeten OF
server.get('/',function(req,res){
	res.send('<h1>Hello, world</h1>');
});

app.use(express.static('public'));
/ en met een public/index.html 

/ Als we de 1ste doen	, dan komt er ook een page terug	, 
<html><head></head><body>Hello, world</body></html>

/ Als we per ongeluk beide doen	, geeft niet	, server.get('/', ...) wint	,

var express=require('express');

	var arr=['Fixes','Movable','Rotating'];
	var str="foo bar"

						block:'Fixes',
						alternative:'Movable',
						other:'Rotating'
	};

/ client-side	,
$ vi public/client.js

$(function(){
	$.get('/blocks',function(blocks){
		var list=[];
		for(var key in blocks){
			var item=$('<li>',{text:blocks[key]});
			list.push(item);
		}
		$('.block-list').append(list);
	});
})

/ Hoeft niet, script staat toch onderin DOM	, 
$(function(){
})

/ 13	. 

/ Als we een JS obj -> JSON	, 
	res.json(obj);	
/ dan zien we de JSON	,	 in devtools	,
{"block":"Fixes","alternative":"Movable","other":"Rotating"}

/ als we 	,
	res.json(arr);

/ level 2, part II

/ logger wordt een module	, want we doen	,

$ vi logger.js
module.exports=function(req,res,next){
	...
	next();
};

/ de logger middleware will be called for each request, and before any of the routes	,
/ next moves the request to the next middleware	,
/ process.stdout is a writable stream	,
/ response is a event emitter. response emits the finished event, when it has completed and the response has been handed to the OS	, so it will be send to the client,	
/ we maken een listener naar dit event,	een callback fct	,  een event handler which runs asynchronously	,

$ vi logger.js

module.exports=function(req,res,next){
	var start=+new Date();
	var stream=process.stdout;
	var url=request.url;
	var method=request.method;
	response.on('finish',function(event){
		var duration=+new Date()-start;
		var message=method+' to '+url+' took '+duration+' ms\n\n';
		stream.write(message);	
	});
	next();
};

/ de event handler is een closure	, want het sluit start, method, duration is , of eig. dus start en request	, 
/ de fct module.exports is allang returned	, 

$ vi index.js

var express=require('express');
var app=express();						

var logger=require('./logger');

app.use(express.static('public'));

app.listen(3000);

	var arr=['Fixes','Movable','Rotating'];
	var str="foo bar"
	var obj={
						block:'Fixes',
						alternative:'Movable',
						other:'Rotating'
	};
	res.json(obj);	
});

$ vi index.js

var express=require('express');
var app=express();						

app.listen(3000);

var blocks={
	Fixed:"Fixed ...",
	Movable:"Movable ...",
	Rotating:"Rotating ..."
};

var locations={
	Fixed:"Fixed +++",
	Movable:"Movable +++", 
	Rotating:"Rotating +++"
};

app.param('name',function(req,res,next){
	var name=req.params.name;	
	var standard=name[0].toUpperCase()+name.slice(1).toLowerCase();
	req.name=standard;
	next();	
});

app.get('/blocks/:name',function(req,res){
	var desc=blocks[req.name];
	if(!desc){
		res.status(404).json("No description found for "+req.params.name+' in blocks');
	}else{
		res.json(desc);	// .json -> 200
	}
});
app.get('/locations/:name',function(req,res){
	var desc=locations[req.name];
	if(!desc){
		res.status(404).json("No description found for "+req.params.name+' in locations');
	}else{
		res.json(desc);	// .json -> 200
	}
});

app.use(express.static('public'));

app.get('/blocks',function(req,res){
  res.json(Object.keys(blocks));
});

/ we doen een POST to /blocks	, pay load (= request body?) name, description
/ we krijgen een 201 Created	, en de name als de response body 

/ we zullen zien dat in de POST request body de text field data url encoded is	, dus de utf-8 bytes staan als STRING er in	, 
/ In de request staan ook utf8 bytes, maar dan binair	,
/ Dus als we Günter echo, dan zien we in de request body %c3%bc	, dan zijn dus 6 char's	, en in het antwoord zien we ü	, dus de bytes c3bc	

/ we deden dit zo snel	,
[eric@almond codeschool]$ echo -n ü | od -t x1
0000000 c3 bc
/ en ü krijgen we door ctrl+shift+u, fc, Enter te geven	,

/ de form's method en action worden hieronder in JS set	,

/ .serialize transforms form data to URL-encoded notation	,

/ form.trigger('reset') triggers de reset event	, het clears de text input fields	,

/ In appendToList	, 
    for(var idx in blockNames){
/ WAS	,
      var item=$('<li>',{text:blockNames[idx]});
/ NU	,
			var content='<a href='/blocks/'+blockNames[idx]+'>'+blockNames[idx]+'</a>';
      var item=$('<li>',{html:content});

/ Bij de POST krijgt .appendToList een array met 1 blockName er in	,

$ vi client.js

$(function(){

	var appendToList=function(blockNames){
		var list=[];
		for(var idx in blockNames){
			var content='<a href="/blocks/'+blockNames[idx]+'">'+blockNames[idx]+'</a>';
      var item=$('<li>',{html:content});
			list.push(item);
		}
		$('.block-list').append(list);
	};
	$.get('/blocks',appendToList);

	$('form').on('submit',function(event){
		event.preventDefault();
		var form=$(this);
		var blockData=form.serialize();
		$.ajax({
			type:'POST',
			url:'/blocks',
			data:blockData
		}).done(function(blockName){
			appendToList([blockName]);
			form.trigger('reset');
		});
	});
})

blockData: "name=Foo&description=Bar%20Baz"

/ extended:false forces the use of the native querystring library	, a query parser	,
/ parseUrlEncoded is een middleware fct	,

app.post('/blocks',parseUrlEncoded,function(req,res){
});
/ routes can take multiple handlers	, worden achter elkaar exec	,

/ using multiple route handlers is reusing middleware that load resources, perform validation, authentication	,

bodyParser.urlencoded(options)
Returns middleware that only parses urlencoded bodies. This parser accepts only UTF-8 encoding of the body and supports automatic inflation of gzip and deflate encodings.

/ Dus body-parses wil utf-8	, in de vorm van dat de utf-8 bytes achter % staan	,

/ Lees	,
http://vim.wikia.com/wiki/Entering_special_characters
ü = utf8 c3bc = unicode 252	=fc 
ε = utf8 ceb5 = unicode 949=03b5 
/ we kunnen in vim	,
^v252			/ ^v kan alleen decimal als <=255
^vu03b5		/ Geef ^v, loslaten, dan u , loslaten, dan 03b5

/ we kunnen in de browser, in een text input	, en in vim, de unicode bytes in hex geven	,
ctrl+shift+u	, loslaten, geef de 2 unicode bytes	, en geef Enter	,
/ ctrl+shift+u, fc (of 00fc)	: ü	 
/ ctrl+shift+u, 03b5	: ε
 

/ Lees	,
https://plus.google.com/+FrancoisBeaufort/posts/gk41YmXWw5J
<Ctrl> + <Shift> + U + 2708 + <Space> = ✈
<Ctrl> + <Shift> + U + 262F + <Space> = ☯
<Ctrl> + <Shift> + U + 2764 + <Space> = ❤ 

/ Geef in chrome	, of in vim	,
^shift u, loslaten	, 03b5	, space, dan zien we ε

/ we kunnen WH ook, 	
Settings, keyboard, shortcuts	, typing , alternative characters key	, kies left alt WH	,

//////////////////////////////
/ Hier staat het allemaal	,
https://help.gnome.org/users/gnome-help/stable/tips-specialchars.html.en

$ vi server.js

app.get('/blocks',function(req,res){
  res.json(Object.keys(blocks));
});
app.post('/blocks',parseUrlEncoded,function(req,res){
  var newBlock=req.body;
  blocks[newBlock.name]=newBlock.description;
  res.status(201).json(newBlock.name);
});

app.get('/blocks/:name',function(req,res){
  var desc=blocks[req.name];
  if(!desc){
    res.status(404).json("No description found for "+req.params.name+' in blocks');
  }else{
    res.json(desc); // .json -> 200
  }
});
app.delete('/blocks/:name',function(req,res){
  delete blocks[req.name];
  res.sendStatus(200);
});

/ we maken	,

$ vi server.js

server.route('/blocks')
.get(function(req,res){
  res.json(Object.keys(blocks));
})
.post(parseUrlEncoded,function(req,res){
  var newBlock=req.body;
  blocks[newBlock.name]=newBlock.description;
  res.status(201).json(newBlock.name);
});

server.route('/blocks/:name')
.get(function(req,res){
  var desc=blocks[req.name];
  if(!desc){
    res.status(404).json("No description found for "+req.params.name+' in blocks');
  }else{
    res.json(desc); // .json -> 200
  }
})
.delete(function(req,res){
  delete blocks[req.name];
  res.sendStatus(200);
});

/ we maken een route tot een module	, bijv de /blocks route	,

$ vi server

var express=require('express');
var server=express();

server.use(express.static('public'));

var router=require('./routes/blocks');	<- router is a middleware	,
server.use('/blocks/',router);					<- router is mounted in a particular root url	,

server.listen(3000);


$ mkdir routes
$ vi routes/blocks.js

var express=require('express');
var router=express.Router();
/ router instance can be mounted as a middleware	,

route.route('/');
/ the root path relative to the path where it is mounted in server.js, server.use('/blocks',...), de path is dus '/blocks'	,
/ we doen dit dus ipv
server.route('/blocks')	
/ , in level4partII	,

module.exports=router;
/ exports the router as a Node module	,

/ 13	. 

/////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////

$ vi icon-toggle-my-fifth/icon-toggle.html

<link rel="import" href="../polymer/polymer.html">
<link rel="import" href="../iron-icon/iron-icon.html">

<link rel="import" href="../iron-icons/communication-icons.html">

<dom-module id="icon-toggle">

  <template>

    <style>
      /* local DOM styles go here */
      :host {
        display: inline-block;
      }
			iron-icon{
				fill:var(--icon-toggle-color,rgba(0,0,0,0));
				stroke: var(--icon-toggle-outline-color, currentcolor);
			}
      :host[pressed] iron-icon {
       	fill: var(--icon-toggle-pressed-color, currentcolor);
			}

    </style>

    <!-- local DOM goes here -->
		<iron-icon icon="polymer" ></iron-icon> 
		<iron-icon icon="communication:email"></iron-icon> 
		<iron-icon icon="[[toggleIcon]]"></iron-icon>
  </template>

  <script>
  Polymer({
   is: "icon-toggle",
    properties: {
      pressed: {
        type: Boolean,
        notify: true,
        reflectToAttribute: true,
        value: false
      },
      toggleIcon: {
        type: String
      },
    },
    listeners: {
      "tap": "toggle",
    },   
    toggle: function() {
      this.pressed = !this.pressed;
    },
  });
  </script>

</dom-module>

		message:function(fav){

				return "You really like me!";

		},

/ 13	. 

/ Het is $ polymer serve	, die die .. handles	,

/ Over import '../polymer/polymer.html'
/ Lees	,
https://www.polymer-project.org/1.0/docs/tools/polymer-cli#element

Bower installs dependencies in a flat dependency tree, like so:

bower_components/
  polymer/
    polymer.html
  my-el/
    my-el.html
  other-el/
    other-el.html
This works well on the application-level. All elements are siblings, so they can all reliably import each other using relative paths like ../polymer/polymer.html. This is why Polymer CLI uses relative paths when initializing your element project.

However, one problem with this approach, as stated earlier, is that this structure does not actually match the layout in your element project. Your element project is actually laid out like so:

bower_components/
  polymer/
    polymer.html
my-el.html
Polymer CLI handles this by remapping paths. When you run polymer serve, all elements in bower_components are remapped to appear to be in sibling directories relative to my-el. The current element is served from the made-up path of /components/bower name, where bower name is the name field from your element project's bower.json file.

			:host{
				display:block;
				padding:16px;
			}
		</style>
		<h1>New view</h1>
	</template>

		Polymer({
			is:"my-new-view",	
			properties:{	
				route:Object
			},
		})
	</script>
</dom-module>

/ video 2.1

/ directive add dynamic behavior to HTML	,
Component: has a template	,
Structural: alters layout, by adding, removing, replacing HTML elements	,
Attributes:  we will not do these 	,


/ 13	. 

/ *ngFor is a structural directive	,


$ vi app/main.ts


import { bootstrap }    from '@angular/platform-browser-dynamic';
import { Component } from '@angular/core';

@Component({
	selector:'my-app',	
	template:`<h1>{{title}}</h1>
		<ul>
			<li *ngFor="let carPart of carParts">
				<h2>{{carPart.name}}</h2>
				<p>{{carPart.description}}</p>
				<p>{{carPart.inStock}} in stock</p>
			</li>
		</ul>`
})
class AppComponent{
	title='Ultra Racing';
	carParts=[
	{
		id:1,
		name:'Super Tires',	
		description:'These tires are the best',	
		inStock:5
	},
	{
		id:2,
		name:'Reinforced shocks',	
		description:'Shocks made from cryptonite',	
		inStock:7
	}
	];
};
bootstrap(AppComponent);

$ vi app/main.ts

import { bootstrap }    from '@angular/platform-browser-dynamic';
import { Component } from '@angular/core';

@Component({
	selector:'my-app',	
	template:`<h1>{{title}}</h1>
		<ul>
			<li *ngFor="let carPart of carParts">
				<h2>{{carPart.name}}</h2>
				<p>{{carPart.description}}</p>
				<p *ngIf="carPart.inStock > 0">{{carPart.inStock}} in stock</p>
				<p *ngIf="carPart.inStock === 0">Out of stock</p>
			</li>
		</ul>`
})
class AppComponent{
	title='Ultra Racing';
	carParts=[

		id:1,

		inStock:5
	},

		description:'Shocks made from cryptonite',	
		inStock:7
	},
	{
		id:3,
		name:'Padded seats',	
		description:'Super ...',	
		inStock:0
	}
	];
};
bootstrap(AppComponent);

$ vi app/main.ts

@Component({
  selector:'my-app',  
  template:`<h1>{{title}}</h1>
    <p>There are {{totalCarParts()}} total car parts in stock</p>
    <ul>
      <li *ngFor="let carPart of carParts">
        <h2>{{carPart.name | uppercase}}</h2>
        <p>{{carPart.description}}</p>
        <p>{{carPart.price | currency:'EUR':true}}</p>
        <p *ngIf="carPart.inStock > 0">{{carPart.inStock}} in stock</p>
        <p *ngIf="carPart.inStock === 0">Out of stock</p>
      </li>
    </ul>`
})
class AppComponent{
  title='Ultra Racing';
  totalCarParts(){
    let sum=0;
    for(let carPart of this.carParts){
      sum+=carPart.inStock;
    }
    return sum;
  };
  carParts=[
  {
    id:1,
    name:'Super Tires',
    description:'These tires are the best',
    inStock:5 ,
    price:4.99
  },
...

import { Component } from '@angular/core';

@Component({
	selector:'car-parts',																									// <-
	template:`																														// <- 
		<p>There are {{totalCarParts()}} total car parts in stock</p>
		<ul>
			<li *ngFor="let carPart of carParts">
				<h2>{{carPart.name | uppercase}}</h2>
				<p>{{carPart.description}}</p>
				<p>{{carPart.price | currency:'EUR':true}}</p>
				<p *ngIf="carPart.inStock > 0">{{carPart.inStock}} in stock</p>
				<p *ngIf="carPart.inStock === 0">Out of stock</p>
			</li>
		</ul>`
})
export class CarPartsComponent{
	totalCarParts(){
		let sum=0;
		for(let carPart of this.carParts){
			sum+=carPart.inStock;
		}
		return sum;
	};
	carParts=[
	{
		id:1,
		name:'Super Tires',	
		description:'These tires are the best',	
		inStock:5	,
		price:4.99
	},
	{
		id:2,
		name:'Reinforced shocks',	
		description:'Shocks made from cryptonite',	
		inStock:7,
		price:5.99
	},
	{
		id:3,
		name:'Padded seats',	
		description:'Super ...',	
		inStock:0,
		price:6.99
	}
	];
};

$ vi app/app.component.ts

import { Component } from '@angular/core';

  selector:'my-app',  
  template:`<h1>{{title}}</h1>
    <car-parts></car-parts>`				// <- our new selector	,

  title='Ultra Racing';
};

/we must tell the AppComponent to explicitly use the CarPartsComponent	,
/ Now Angular does not know yet to look for our car-parts selector inside the template	, hij weet niet waar deze is	,
/ TODO
/ we need to tell AppComponent we are using CarPartsComponent in the template	,

$ vi app/app.component.ts

import { Component } from '@angular/core';
import {CarPartsComponent} from './car-parts.component';

@Component({
  selector:'my-app',  
  template:` <h1>{{title}}</h1>
    <car-parts></car-parts> `,
  directives:[ CarPartsComponent ];
})
export class AppComponent{
  title='Ultra Racing';
};

@Component({
  selector:'car-parts',
  template:` 
    <p>There are {{totalCarParts()}} total car parts in stock</p>
    <ul>
      <li *ngFor="let carPart of carParts">
        <h2>{{carPart.name | uppercase}}</h2>
        <p class='description'>{{carPart.description}}</p>
        <p class='price'>{{carPart.price | currency:'EUR':true}}</p>
        <p *ngIf="carPart.inStock > 0">{{carPart.inStock}} in stock</p>
        <p *ngIf="carPart.inStock === 0">Out of stock</p>
      </li>
    </ul>`,
  styles:[`
    .description{
      color:red;
      font-size:small;
    }
    .price{
      font-weight:bold;
    }`
  ]

$ vi app/car-part.component.ts

import { Component } from '@angular/core';
import {CarPart}from './car-part';					// <-
import {CARPARTS}from './mocks';						// <-

@Component({
	selector:'car-parts',	
	templateUrl:'app/car-parts.component.html',
	styleUrls:['app/car-parts.component.css']
})
export class CarPartsComponent{
	totalCarParts(){
		let sum=0;
		for(let carPart of this.carParts){
			sum+=carPart.inStock;
		}
		return sum;
	};
	carParts:CarPart[];										// <- 	does nothing TODO
	ngOnInit(){
		this.carParts=CARPARTS;
	};
};

/ OK

/ De line
	carParts:CarPart[];										// <- 	does nothing TODO
/ does nothing	, 
 /we can write
	carParts:CrPart[];										
/ we can rename the properties in CarPart in car-part.ts , or given another type, it all does not matter	,
/ also when we had `...` here	, 
	carParts:CarPart[]=`...`	
/ the same	,

/ de {{ en }} moeten tussen '...'	, 

/ of we doen	,
        <img [src]='carPart.image'>

/ property binding: glue component properties to DOM element properties	,

/ we kunnen ook	, 
<div [hidden]='!user.isAdmin'>secret</div>
<button [disable]='isDisabled'>Purchase</button>
<img [alt]='image.description'>

/  property binding is 1-way binding: van component property -> DOM element property	,

				<h2>{{carPart.name | uppercase}}</h2>
				<p class='description'>{{carPart.description}}</p>
				<p class='price'>{{carPart.price | currency:'EUR':true}}</p>
				<p *ngIf="carPart.inStock > 0">{{carPart.inStock}} in stock</p>
				<p *ngIf="carPart.inStock === 0">Out of stock</p>
			</li>
		</ul>

if carPart.featured=true, the featured class is added	, 
if carPart.featured=false, the featured class is removed,

$ vi app/car-parts.component.ts

import { Component } from '@angular/core';
import {CarPart}from './car-part';
import {CARPARTS}from './mocks';

@Component({
  selector:'car-parts',
  templateUrl:'app/car-parts.component.html',
  styleUrls:['app/car-parts.component.css']
})
export class CarPartsComponent{
  totalCarParts(){
    let sum=0;
    for(let carPart of this.carParts){
      sum+=carPart.inStock;
    }
    return sum;
  };
  carParts:CarPart[];
  ngOnInit(){
    this.carParts=CARPARTS;
  };
  upQuantity(){
    alert('up quantity!');
  };
}

/ to capture an event from our template, we wrap the name of the event we want to listen to in parenthesis and specify the method to call	,

/ 13	. 

/ Any standard DOM event can be listened for by wrapping it in parenthesis and removing the 'on' at the beginning of the word	,

<div (mouseover)='call()'>
<input (blur)='call()'>
<input(focus)='call()'>
<input type="text" (keydown)='call()'>
<form (submit)='call'>

/ 13	. 

/ Sometimes you need additional data, like which key is pressed or where the mouse is on the screen. This is what the Angular event object is for	,

/ we can also call event.preventDefault()	, to prevent a link being followed, or a form being submitted. 

$ vi app/car-parts.component.html
       <div>
          <input type="text" (keydown)='showKey($event)'>
          <h2 (mouseover)='getCoord($event)'>Enter me</h2>
        </div>

$ vi app/car-parts.component.ts
...
export class CarPartsComponent{
  showKey(event){
    console.log(event.keyCode);
  }
  getCoord(event){
    console.log(event.clientX+','+event.clientY);
  }
}


/ video 4.7	,

/ (class ) property binding : 1-way JS -> HTML : een property (attr, class) verschijnt in  HTML of niet	, 
/ event binding: 1-way HTML-> JS : een click event gebeurt in HTML en de handler is in JS	,

/////////////////////
/ een voorbeeld van een property is de value property van een text input in een form	,

/ hoe 2-way, bijv een text field in een form	, dat als je in HTML text ingeeft	, dat deze naar JS gaat, maar ook dat als in JS de value verandert, dat in de form ook gebeurt	, 

/ 13	. 

/ we maken een text input naat + en - buttons	, en laten de value load met die uit JS	, die met events in JS zijn set	, 
/ dus 
/ 1-way: +/- : HTML -> JS
/ 1-way: JS-> HTML : set value in input met die in JS staat	,


$ vi app/car-parts.component.html

        <div>
          {{carPart.quantity}}
          <button (click)='upQuantity(carPart)'>+</button>
          <button (click)='downQuantity(carPart)'>-</button>
          <input type='text' [value]='carPart.quantity'>					<-
        </div>

/ nogmaals: wat +/-  met events naar JS sturen, laten we set in input field	,

/ Nu willen we een getal geven in input, en dat naar JS sturen	, 
/ Dus vanuit +/- en vanuit de input -> JS

/ 2-way binding van input 	,

$ vi app/car-parts.component.html

        <div>
          {{carPart.quantity}}
          <button (click)='upQuantity(carPart)'>+</button>
          <button (click)='downQuantity(carPart)'>-</button>
          <input type='text' [value]='carPart.quantity' (input)='carPart.quantity=$event.target.value'>
        </div>

/ OK
/ we hoeven alleen 3 bijv. in te type in de input	, Enter of zoiets is niet nodig	,

/ Maar het kan ook zo	, 2-way binding van input	,

$ vi app/car-parts.component.html

       <div>
          {{carPart.quantity}}
          <button (click)='upQuantity(carPart)'>+</button>
          <button (click)='downQuantity(carPart)'>-</button>
          <input type='text' [(ngModel)]='carPart.quantity' >
        </div>
